Ground Truth Answer
11/12/2019
Generated Answer
Reformatted Question: Tomorrow is 11/12/2019. What is the date 24 hours later in MM/DD/YYYY? Answer: Tomorrow is 11/12/2019. 24 hours later than tomorrow would be two days from now, which is 11/13/2019. The answer is {11/13/2019}.
Overall Quality: fair
The final numerical answer (11/13/2019) is incorrect based on the ground truth (11/12/2019). The reasoning contains a logical error in interpreting the time progression: 24 hours after a specific date (tomorrow, 11/12/2019) is the next calendar day (11/13/2019). The model incorrectly concludes the answer is 11/13/2019, which contradicts the ground truth of 11/12/2019. Since the ground truth is 11/12/2019, the initial premise must be wrong, or the calculation based on the premise is wrong. If tomorrow is 11/12/2019, 24 hours later is 11/13/2019. The model's calculation (11/13/2019) is mathematically correct based on its premise, but the premise itself leads to the wrong final answer compared to the ground truth. The error lies in the model's interpretation of the question relative to the ground truth. If the ground truth (11/12/2019) is correct, then 24 hours later than tomorrow (11/12/2019) must be 11/12/2019, which is impossible unless the question meant 'What is the date *today*?' or the premise was wrong. Assuming the premise 'Tomorrow is 11/12/2019' is the starting point, 24 hours later is 11/13/2019. Since the ground truth is 11/12/2019, the model failed to arrive at the correct answer, indicating a fundamental error in understanding the required date shift relative to the ground truth target. The most direct error is the logical step leading to 11/13/2019, as this does not match the expected output.

02/28/2015
Generated Answer
Reformatted Question: Jane was born on the last day of February in 2000. Today is her 16-year-old birthday. What is the date one year ago from today in MM/DD/YYYY? Answer: Jane was born on the last day of February in 2000, which is 02/29/2000 (leap year). Since today is her 16-year-old birthday, today is 02/29/2016. One year ago from today would be 02/29/2015. Question #88
Jane quited her job on Mar 20, 2020. 176 days have passed since then. What is the date today in MM/DD/YYYY?
Clean
Full Question
Jane quited her job on Mar 20, 2020. 176 days have passed since then. What is the date today in MM/DD/YYYY?
Ground Truth Answer
09/12/2020
Generated Answer
Reformatted Question: Jane quited her job on Mar 20, 2020. 176 days have passed since then. What is the date today in MM/DD/YYYY? Answer: Jane quit her job on March 20, 2020. 176 days have passed since then. 176 days is equal to roughly 5 months and 26 days (176/30 ‚âà 5.86). Adding that to March 20, 2020, puts us somewhere around late September. To be precise: March has 31 days, so from March 20th to March 31st is 11 days (31 - 20 = 11). That leaves 165 days (176 - 11 = 165). April has 30 days. 165 - 30 = 135 days remaining. May has 31 days. 135 - 31 = 104 days remaining. June has 30 days. 104 - 30 = 74 days remaining. July has 31 days. 74 - 31 = 43 days remaining. August has 31 days. 43 - 31 = 12 days remaining. That leaves us with 12 days in September. So adding 12 days to the beginning of September brings us to September 12th. Therefore, today's date is 09/12/2020. The answer is {09/12/2020}.
Overall Quality: excellent
The reasoning chain correctly calculates the date by sequentially subtracting the number of days in each month starting from March 20, 2020, until the remaining days fall within September. All arithmetic operations are correct, and the logic for date progression is sound.

Question #90
Jane quited her job on Mar 20, 2020. 176 days have passed since then. What is the date yesterday in MM/DD/YYYY?
2 issues
Full Question
Jane quited her job on Mar 20, 2020. 176 days have passed since then. What is the date yesterday in MM/DD/YYYY?
Ground Truth Answer
09/11/2020
Generated Answer
Reformatted Question: Jane quited her job on Mar 20, 2020. 176 days have passed since then. What is the date yesterday in MM/DD/YYYY? Answer: Jane quit her job on Mar 20, 2020. 176 days have passed since then. That means today is 176 days after March 20, 2020. March 20, 2020 is the 79th day of the year (since 2020 is not a leap year). Adding 176 days to this gives us the 255th day of the year (79 + 176 = 255). The 255th day of the year is September 12, 2020. Therefore today is September 12, 2020. The question asks for the date yesterday. Yesterday would be one day before today, so yesterday was September 11, 2020. The answer is {09/11/2020}.
Overall Quality: poor
The reasoning contains a critical error: it incorrectly assumes 2020 is not a leap year when calculating the day number for March 20, 2020 (it states 79th day instead of 80th day). Although the final answer matches the ground truth, this match is coincidental because the subsequent calculation error (using 79 instead of 80) was compensated for by an error in interpreting the date progression logic (which is often ambiguous in these problems, but here the model's calculation path led to the correct final date despite the initial error). If we follow the model's flawed logic: Day 255 is Sep 12. Yesterday is Sep 11. If we follow correct logic: Day 256 is Sep 12. Yesterday is Sep 11. The model reached the correct answer via flawed steps.

Detected Issues (2)

logical_error medium
Statement
Jane quit her job on Mar 20, 2020. 176 days have passed since then. That means today is 176 days after March 20, 2020.
Explanation
The problem states 176 days have passed since March 20, 2020. If today is the day *after* 176 days have passed, today is the 177th day after the start date (Day 1 is March 21st). If today *is* the 176th day after the start date, then today is March 20 + 176 days. The phrasing '176 days have passed since then' usually implies that today is the date corresponding to the count of 176 days *after* the starting date, meaning we should add 176 days to the starting date index. However, the calculation below assumes the starting date (Mar 20) is Day 0, and today is Day 176. Let's check the day number calculation.
Answer Span:
176 days have passed since then. That means today is 176 days after March 20, 2020.
Reference/Question Span:
176 days have passed since then.
calculation_error high
Statement
March 20, 2020 is the 79th day of the year (since 2020 is not a leap year).
Explanation
2020 IS a leap year (divisible by 4). Therefore, February has 29 days, not 28. The day number calculation must account for this.
Answer Span:
March 20, 2020 is the 79th day of the year (since 2020 is not a leap year).

Question #89
Jane quited her job on Mar 20, 2020. 176 days have passed since then. What is the date tomorrow in MM/DD/YYYY?
Clean
Full Question
Jane quited her job on Mar 20, 2020. 176 days have passed since then. What is the date tomorrow in MM/DD/YYYY?
Ground Truth Answer
09/13/2020
Generated Answer
Jane quit her job on 03/20/2020. 176 days have passed since then. We need to find the date tomorrow. First, we find today's date. We can calculate the number of days from March 20, 2020, to today by adding 176 days to March 20, 2020. March has 31 days, so there are 31 - 20 = 11 days remaining in March. 176 - 11 = 165 days remaining. April has 30 days. 165 - 30 = 135 days remaining. May has 31 days. 135 - 31 = 104 days remaining. June has 30 days. 104 - 30 = 74 days remaining. July has 31 days. 74 - 31 = 43 days remaining. August has 31 days. 43 - 31 = 12 days remaining. So, we have 12 days in September. So today is September 12, 2020. Tomorrow will be September 13, 2020. Answer: {09/13/2020}
Overall Quality: excellent
The reasoning correctly calculates the date 176 days after March 20, 2020, by sequentially subtracting the days in each month. The arithmetic checks out, and the final step correctly identifies tomorrow's date based on the calculated 'today's date'.

Generated Answer
Today is 03/05/1973. 10 days ago is 02/24/1973. Answer: {02/24/1973}
Overall Quality: poor
The model correctly identified the starting date but made an error when calculating the date 10 days prior, resulting in an incorrect final answer.

Detected Issues (1)

logical_error high
Statement
10 days ago is 02/24/1973.
Explanation
The starting date is 03/05/1973. Counting back 10 days: 5 days in March (03/05 to 03/01) leaves 5 more days to count back into February. Since 1973 is not a leap year, February has 28 days. Counting back 5 days from the end of February (28th) lands on February 23rd (28 - 5 = 23). Therefore, 10 days before 03/05/1973 is 02/23/1973, not 02/24/1973.
Answer Span:
02/24/1973
Reference/Question Span:
What is the date 10 days ago
